Overview Notes: A raised usCRP is considered a risk factor for cardiac and other chronic disease, however your result would have been affected by the infection in your elbow. Repeat the level once the elbow has fully resolved.
Comment Key: ClinicalExamComment
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Type II diabetic, low free testosterone, mild obstruction on lung function (ex smoker)

Overview Notes: Losing weight, especially around your abdomen will help to control yout diabetes and decrease your risk of chronic disease in general. The dietitian can guide you with an appropriate eating plan and you can increase your exercise to 30 minutes at least 5 times per week. Stress management is also important.
Comment Key: CurrentComplaintRecommendation

Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Blood sugar control can be disturbed by infection (your recent elbow infection) and hence could be why your fasting glucose was a bit raised. Please recheck your fasting blood glucose level now that the infection has resolved and if still raised discuss management with Dr Skye, including lifestyle management and possible medication adjustment.
Comment Key: EyesightRecommendation
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Type II diabetic, low free testosterone, mild obstruction on lung function (ex smoker)

Overview Notes: Homocysteine can also increase the risk of heart disease. Supplementing with active B vitamins such as in Phytomulti or a high quality B supplement can help to lower this level.
Comment Key: LifestyleNote
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Type II diabetic, low free testosterone, mild obstruction on lung function (ex smoker)

Clinical Recommendations: 
Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Blood sugar control can be disturbed by infection (your recent elbow infection) and hence could be why your fasting glucose was a bit raised. Please recheck your fasting blood glucose level now that the infection has resolved and if still raised discuss management with Dr Skye, including lifestyle management and possible medication adjustment.
Comment Key: LifestyleRecommendation
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Type II diabetic, low free testosterone, mild obstruction on lung function (ex smoker)

Employee: Simon Woodward
Report Date: 2020-02-11
Doctor: Christie Pilossof
Nurse: Lebo Cindi
Clinical Recommendations: Normal examination. Borderline BP - please monitor.
Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Blood sugar control can be disturbed by infection (your recent elbow infection) and hence could be why your fasting glucose was a bit raised. Please recheck your fasting blood glucose level now that the infection has resolved and if still raised discuss management with Dr Skye, including lifestyle management and possible medication adjustment.

Nurse: Lebo Cindi

Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.

Employee: Simon Woodward

Doctor: Christie Pilossof
Nurse: Lebo Cindi
Clinical Recommendations: 
Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Blood sugar control can be disturbed by infection (your recent elbow infection) and hence could be why your fasting glucose was a bit raised. Please recheck your fasting blood glucose level now that the infection has resolved and if still raised discuss management with Dr Skye, including lifestyle management and possible medication adjustment.

Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Blood sugar control can be disturbed by infection (your recent elbow infection) and hence could be why your fasting glucose was a bit raised. Please recheck your fasting blood glucose level now that the infection has resolved and if still raised discuss management with Dr Skye, including lifestyle management and possible medication adjustment.
Comment Key: MentalHealthNote
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Type II diabetic, low free testosterone, mild obstruction on lung function (ex smoker)

Comment Key: ReportRecommendation
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Type II diabetic, low free testosterone, mild obstruction on lung function (ex smoker)
------------------------------
Employee: Simon Woodward
Report Date: 2020-02-11
Doctor: Christie Pilossof
Nurse: Lebo Cindi
Clinical Recommendations: 
Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Blood sugar control can be disturbed by infection (your recent elbow infection) and hence could be why your fasting glucose was a bit raised. Please recheck your fasting blood glucose level now that the infection has resolved and if still raised discuss management with Dr Skye, including lifestyle management and possible medication adjustment.

Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Losing weight, especially around your abdomen will help to control yout diabetes and decrease your risk of chronic disease in general. The dietitian can guide you with an appropriate eating plan and you can increase your exercise to 30 minutes at least 5 times per week. Stress management is also important.
Comment Key: SpecialInvestigationRecommendation
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Type II diabetic, low free testosterone, mild obstruction on lung function (ex smoker)

Nurse: Lebo Cindi
Clinical Recommendations: 
Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Losing weight, especially around your abdomen will help to control yout diabetes and decrease your risk of chronic disease in general. Men's Health Recommendations: You saw the urologist last year and he was happy.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: A raised usCRP is considered a risk factor for cardiac and other chronic disease, however your result would have been affected by the infection in your elbow. Repeat the level once the elbow has fully resolved.
Comment Key: WomensHealthNote
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Type II diabetic, low free testosterone, mild obstruction on lung function (ex smoker)

Overview Notes: Losing weight, especially around your abdomen will help to control yout diabetes and decrease your risk of chronic disease in general. The dietitian can guide you with an appropriate eating plan and you can increase your exercise to 30 minutes at least 5 times per week. Stress management is also important.
